	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php');
	writefile_17();
	if (!is_file('plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php') != 'b271d90e9c6b96738e75094be4c60e8b9bd0691d') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php') !== 'b271d90e9c6b96738e75094be4c60e8b9bd0691d') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php') !== '8d3f62bbe9f85152528e9e5fb53c3fb7ce52e372') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_17();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php') !== 'b271d90e9c6b96738e75094be4c60e8b9bd0691d') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php');
	writefile_18();
	if (!is_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php') != 'de67d176dd659873601ee1b417752bc19a7fe6b4') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php') !== 'de67d176dd659873601ee1b417752bc19a7fe6b4') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php') !== '370a7a63e44ad1beee2bd9c51d14ef5c2fc3a090') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_18();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php') !== 'de67d176dd659873601ee1b417752bc19a7fe6b4') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/doi/plugin.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/objectTypes/other/plugin.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_25();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/other/plugin.inc.php') !== '320a78dc75bdf11c5b9e438489a79be512dcb40f') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/other/plugin.inc.php');
